NOTE TO THE CANDIDATES 
 
1. The tuition fee will be collected as per Governmentnorms. 
 
2. The hostel charges and transportation charges are given in this booklet.  The 
candidates are advised to note these charges before making achoice. 
3. Request for change from one college to another or change of branch will 
not beentertained. 
4. Some of the colleges have not furnished complete information. Those 
colleges may be contacted directly, if the candidates sodesire. 
5. The courses/branches indicated in this booklet are based on the information 
given by the respective colleges. Any change in the existing branches/intake 
or if approval is obtained from the competent authority for changes intake 
in the existing branches on for any new branches in colleges before the 
commencement of counseling, such of those details will be verified in the 
Affiliating University web portal. It is the responsibility of the candidates to 
note carefully such additional information before exercising their option for 
the college andbranch. 
6. Mere inclusion in the booklet does not entitle the college to be included in 
the single window counseling for TNEA2022. 
iii 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
The details given in this booklet are as received 
from the colleges concerned as on 17-07-2023. 
Changes if any, will be uploaded in the web portal

TAMIL NADU ENGINEERING ADMISSIONS 2023 
CHOICE PREPARATION SHEET FOR B.E/B.TECH. COURSES 
 
Note: Choice is a branch in college / institution. Choices should be prepared in the order of 
applicant’s preferences. Order of applicant’s preferences is the applicant’s the applicant’s priority of 
choices for allotment ordered from most preferred to least. For example, Choice Number 1 will be 
considered as the most preferred choice for allotment. If Choice number 1 could not be allotted based 
on merit list, then choice number 2,3,…so on (in strict order) will be considered for allotment based 
on merit list. Hence, prepare the ordered choice list carefully. Take multiple copies of this form is 
required.
